Changelog

Date Author Change
2017-02-14 Lubomir Rintel <lkundrak at v3 dot sk> - 1:4.0.6-1.3 - Update to 4.0.6
2015-07-09 Lubomir Rintel <lkundrak at v3 dot sk> - 2015.03.21-2.rev5528.1 - Do with a bit older Boost for el7 - Only build on Intel -- no boost-context elsewhere for the Boost version in el7
2015-04-14 Marcin Juszkiewicz <mjuszkiewicz at redhat dot com> - 2015.03.21-2.rev5528 - Handle all 64-bit architectures
2015-03-22 Lubomir Rintel <lkundrak at v3 dot sk> - 2015.03.21-1.rev5528 - Update to a later snapshot - Fix the freerouter patch - Enable parallel build
2015-03-19 Lubomir Rintel <lkundrak at v3 dot sk> - 2015.02.05-1.rev5404 - Update to a later snapshot
2015-01-27 Petr Machata <pmachata at redhat dot com> - 2014.03.13-11.rev4744 - Rebuild for boost 1.57.0 - Add upstream patch to support new Boost.Context API (kicad-2014.03.13-boost-context.patch)
2015-01-02 Lubomir Rintel <lkundrak at v3 dot sk> - 2014.03.13-10.rev4744 - Use local autorouter
2014-11-30 Lubomir Rintel <lkundrak at v3 dot sk> - 2014.03.13-9.rev4744 - Install library footprints
2014-08-18 Rex Dieter <rdieter at fedoraproject dot org> 2014.03.13-8.rev4744 - update mime scriptlets
2014-08-17 Fedora Release Engineering <rel dash eng at lists dot fedoraproject dot org> - 2014.03.13-7.rev4744 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_21_22_Mass_Rebuild
